class="article-ga-wrap" data-reactid="190"><header class="article-header" data-reactid="191"><h1 class="story-title story-title__article" itemprop="headline" data-reactid="192">Puma Made $975 Million Last Quarter Thanks to Rihanna&#x27;s Sneakers</h1><!-- react-text: 193 --><!-- /react-text --><div class="info-row clearfix" data-reactid="194"><div class="info-row__credits" data-reactid="195"><div     </div></div></div><figcaption class="lead-carousel__caption lead-carousel__caption--center" data-reactid="219">Video via Complex News</figcaption><a href="http://www.youtube.com/user/complexmagazine?sub_confirmation=1" target="_blank" class="fenix-button gtm-click subscribe-button subscribe-button--youtube gtm-social" data-gtm-module="SubscribeButton" data-gtm-module-location="Lead Carousel" data-gtm-social-site="Youtube" data-reactid="220"><i class="cmplx-icon icon-youtube" data-reactid="221"></i><!-- react-text: 222 --> Subscribe On <!-- /react-text --><!-- react-text: 223 -->youtube<!-- /react-text --></a></figure><!-- react-empty: 224 --><div class="article-body" itemprop="articleBody" data-reactid="225"><div class="article__copy clearfix" data-reactid="226"><p data-reactid="227">Towards the end of 2014, Puma surprised sneakerheads by <a target="_self" href="http://www.complex.com/sneakers/2014/12/female-sneakerhead-reactions-rihanna-puma-creative-director/">naming Rihanna</a> its women&apos;s creative director, and now a little over a year later, it looks like the move has paid off big time.</p><p data-reactid="228"><a target="_blank" href="http://www.bloomberg.com/news/articles/2016-02-18/puma-profit-tops-estimates-as-rihanna-designed-shoes-boost-sales"><em>Bloomberg Business</em></a>&#xA0;reports that Puma&apos;s 2015 fourth quarter earnings managed to surpass analyst predictions with &#x20AC;879 million (roughly $975 million) in sales, which are up 17.1 percent from fourth quarter 2014 and far beyond expert projections of&#xA0;<span>&#x20AC;847.9 million.&#xA0;</span></p><p data-reactid="229"><span>According to the brand, the sales surge is due in large part to its <a target="_self" href="http://www.complex.com/style/2015/11/rihanna-puma-sales-increase">sneaker collaborations with Rihanna</a>, and Puma CEO&#xA0;Bjoern Gulden added that Rihanna &quot;can sell sneakers and Puma is onto something here which we haven&apos;t seen yet in the women&apos;s area.&quot;</span></p><p data-reactid="230">Next up from the Rihanna x Puma collaboration is the Fenty&#xA0;line, which <a target="_self" href="http://www.complex.com/style/2016/02/rihanna-fenty-puma-mens-looks-nyfw">made its debut last week</a> at New York Fashion Week. Meanwhile, we can only imagine that Puma&apos;s <a target="_self" href="http://www.complex.com/sneakers/2016/02/puma-kylie-jenner-confirmation">just-announced Kylie Jenner partnership</a> will help to further bolster sales. Stay tuned.&#xA0;</p></div></div></div></div><!-- react-empty: 231 --><div class="lazyload-placeholder" data-reactid="232"></div><div class="article-tags article-tags--margins clearfix" They were both hit with double technical fouls and sent packing. It came after Thomas scored just 3 points in 5 minutes of action.\\u003C\\u002Fp\\u003E\\n\\n\\u003Cp\\u003EAfter the game, Thomas was asked about what happened between him and Rondo, and he seemed as confused as everyone else about it. Thomas suggested Rondo targeted him from the moment he checked into the game, and he claimed Rondo hit him in the face several times while also taunting him about the tribute video the Celtics had planned to play for him prior to a game when he was still playing with the Cavaliers. Even though Thomas played a part in getting the Celtics to change their plans to play the tribute video since they were thinking about doing it on the same night as Paul Pierce’s jersey retirement ceremony, Thomas said Rondo still seemed upset it was scheduled in the first place.\\u003C\\u002Fp\\u003E\\n\\n\\u003Cp\\u003E“He’s an upset guy about me. I don’t know what it’s for, but it’s fine. He kept bringing the tribute up, when I was the one that shut the tribute down. I’m far past that…For me to be ejected was uncalled for.”\\u003C\\u002Fp\\u003E\\n\\n\\u003Cp\\u003EThomas was asked by reporters if he and Rondo have any bad blood as a result of anything else that happened in the past. Thomas said he couldn’t think of any reason why Rondo would dislike him, but he did bring up the fact that Thomas and the Celtics knocked off Rondo and the Bulls in the playoffs last season.\\u003C\\u002Fp\\u003E\\n\\n\\u003Cp\\u003E\\\"I mean, my team beat his team in the playoffs last year. Maybe that is what&#39;s wrong. I don&#39;t know. There&#39;s nothing. Nothing should&#39;ve made that escalate like it did. He already had his agenda written down right when I checked into the game. It was obvious. He picked me up full court, trying to be physical.”\\u003C\\u002Fp\\u003E\\n\\n\\u003Cp\\u003EThomas also let it be known that he didn’t feel as though he should have been ejected from the game. He blamed the game’s officials for letting Rondo take things too far and said he plans on trying to get the league to rescind the technical fouls that were given to him.\\u003C\\u002Fp\\u003E\\n\\n\\u003Cp\\u003E\\\"It felt like they were waiting for me to get upset. I got hit in the face three times, and the third time I got hit in my face, I reacted and tried to tell the refs, &#39;Are you guys going to control this?&#39; I definitely need to get those technical fouls rescinded.\\\"\\u003C\\u002Fp\\u003E\\n\\n\\u003Cp\\u003ERondo didn’t speak with the media after the game, so he didn’t get a chance to tell his side of the story. But if he did, in fact, taunt Thomas over the tribute video the Celtics planned for him, it wouldn’t be all that surprising. After a Pelicans game in January, Rondo was asked about the video, and he said he didn’t understand why Boston was going to honor Thomas.\\u003C\\u002Fp\\u003E\\n\\n\\u003Cp\\u003E“What has he done?”\\u003C\\u002Fp\\u003E\\n\\n\\u003Cp\\u003ERondo also had a response for a reporter who suggested Thomas deserved a tribute video for leading the Celtics to the Eastern Conference Finals in 2017.\\u003C\\u002Fp\\u003E\\n\\n\\u003Cp\\u003E“Oh, that’s what we celebrate around here?”\\u003C\\u002Fp\\u003E\\n\\n\\u003Cp\\u003EFor those who might be wondering, the Lakers and Pelicans are scheduled to play one more time this season. They will meet in New Orleans on March 22. It’ll be interesting to see if Thomas and Rondo have cooled off by then or if they decide to go at it again when they take the court. After what took place on Wednesday, it wouldn’t be a shock to see them butt heads for a second time when the two teams match up.\\u003C\\u002Fp\\u003E\\n\\n\\u003Cp\\u003EThat’s the news for now, but for all of the latest news on the NBA, subscribe to Complex News on YouTube. If you count Nostalgia, Ultra as an album then most would say Frank fell one short of his goal.\\u003C\\u002Fp\\u003E\\n\\n\\u003Cp\\u003E\\u003Cbr \\u002F\\u003E\\nBut Frank took to Tumblr late last year and said “Well I made the album before 30. I just ain’t put that bitch out.”\\u003C\\u002Fp\\u003E\\n\\n\\u003Cp\\u003E\\u003Cbr \\u002F\\u003E\\nSo, will he? There’s absolutely no reason to take Moon River as a suggestion that he’s ready to drop another project, but hey, it’s February. The year is still young enough for us to project a lot of impossible wishes onto it. up, guys? Frazier here for Complex News.\\u003C\\u002Fp\\u003E\\n\\n\\u003Cp\\u003EIt’s been less than a year since Aaron Hernandez took his own life while sitting behind bars on a murder conviction. But it sounds like there’s already a rush to turn Hernandez’s life story into a movie at some point in the near future. And it appears as though it’s causing some trouble in Hollywood, where at least one person is allegedly going to great lengths to stop a company from making a movie.\\u003C\\u002Fp\\u003E\\n\\n\\u003Cp\\u003EIn January, The Mark Gordon Entertainment Co. acquired the feature film rights to the book All-American Murder: The Rise and Fall of Aaron Hernandez, the Superstar Whose Life Ended on Murderer’s Row, a book by James Patterson and Alex Abramovich. The plan was to use the rights to turn the book, which dissects the rise and fall of Hernandez, into a movie.\\u003C\\u002Fp\\u003E\\n\\n\\u003Cp\\u003EHowever, shortly after news about the company obtaining the feature film rights to the book broke, a man named Todd Guzze allegedly started harassing the company’s employees and going as far as to make gang threats while corresponding with them through email. According to Deadline, Guzze is apparently working on an Aaron Hernandez project of his own, and in an email he sent to Mark Gordon Entertainment Co. employee Josh Clay Phillips, Guzze allegedly suggested the Bloods and Latin Kings gangs were helping him make it. He also used his alleged gang affiliation to direct a threat at Phillips and the rest of the Mark Gordon Co. staff.\\u003C\\u002Fp\\u003E\\n\\n\\u003Cp\\u003E“I don’t need to tell you how they work…I’m keeping them at bay right now, they don’t even know this is going on at this second. So that’s my last little tidbit for you, and they’re right here in L.A.”\\u003C\\u002Fp\\u003E\\n\\n\\u003Cp\\u003EGuzze allegedly attached a photo of several men holding guns to his email to Phillips. Guzze also reportedly sent him a photo of Phillips and his wife that was on Phillips’ Facebook page and asked, “Is this you? From Aaron Hernandez?” He allegedly added: “Are you ready?” and “I hope it’s worth it.”\\u003C\\u002Fp\\u003E\\n\\n\\u003Cp\\u003EIn addition to allegedly sending threats in Phillips’ direction, Guzze has also reportedly threatened to take legal action against Mark Gordon Entertainment Co. if they follow through on their plan to turn the Hernandez book into a movie. He got in touch with the Mark Gordon Entertainment Co. and the general counsel for the Machete Book Group after hearing about the plan and initially offered to partner with them on the movie. But towards the end of their correspondence, Guzze reportedly made another threat.\\u003C\\u002Fp\\u003E\\n\\n\\u003Cp\\u003E“You want it, I’m right here. I’ll give it to you. If you ignore me, or try to play HOLLYWOOD EGO games, I’ll implode it.”\\u003C\\u002Fp\\u003E\\n\\n\\u003Cp\\u003EThe Santa Monica Police Department’s Criminal Investigations Division is now looking into the alleged threats Guzze made to Mark Gordon Entertainment Co.\\u003C\\u002Fp\\u003E\\n\\n\\u003Cp\\u003EDeadline reached out to Guzze to discuss the alleged threats this week, and he seemed to respond to the allegations made against him by calling them “guerrilla marketing techniques.” He also suggested he was simply trying to get the attention of the Mark Gordon Entertainment Co. when he first started contacting them.\\u003C\\u002Fp\\u003E\\n\\n\\u003Cp\\u003E“The Entertainment Industry is big business, and it usually lacks a sense of humor. We’ve had to use guerrilla marketing techniques, at times, in order to get some people’s attention. We’re not the first ones to do it, and we won’t be the last. This is not about Aaron Hernandez, Natalie Wood, or Emmett Till. This is about a group of artists, some minority, that have worked really hard to get to this point, and are just looking for a specific window of opportunity to shine, or be recognized.”\\u003C\\u002Fp\\u003E\\n\\n\\u003Cp\\u003EWhile police try to make sense of exactly what’s going on here, the Mark Gordon Entertainment Co. has filed a restraining order against Guzze and asked a court to get him to leave their employees alone. A hearing is scheduled to take place on March 1 on the matter.\\u003C\\u002Fp\\u003E\\n\\n\\u003Cp\\u003EThat’s the news for now, but for all of the latest news on Aaron Hernandez, subscribe to Complex News on YouTube.
